		function active_tab() {


			var d = new Date();
	        var s = d.getSeconds();
	        var hs = 0;
	        var slot = 10;
	        var mytab = 1;
	        if (isNaN(s) == false) {
	                hs = s % (slot - 1);
	                mytab = (hs < 9) ? 1 : 2;
	        }
	        new Yetii({ id: 'box-ilmiolibro', active: mytab});

		}
